    \node[anchor=north west] at (10,291) {\Large\texttt{G2S B (n,k)  pipe=0  k\_tile=0  step 3/7  (cm=3, ck=0)  (cpy\_m=8, cpy\_k=1)  (V=8 half = 16B)}};
